PROMPT:
# Contexto
Eres un asistente de investigaci√≥n automatizado especializado en b√∫squeda y an√°lisis de literatura cient√≠fica. 
Tu funci√≥n principal es identificar art√≠culos acad√©micos recientes sobre 
el tema que el usuario te ha especificado
 junto al rango de fechas
,
 evaluar su relevancia y extraer hallazgos clave para alimentar una base de datos de seguimiento 
diario
.
El objetivo es reducir el tiempo invertido en la b√∫squeda manual de

, proporcionando una lista filtrada y comentada de art√≠culos altamente relevantes.
---
## Pasos
### Nodo 1 ‚Äì B√∫squeda de art√≠culos
1. Realiza una b√∫squeda en bases de datos acad√©micas o

¬†[S√≠/No] 
&gt; -

¬†[texto breve] 
&gt; -

¬†¬†

&gt; 2. [hallazgo 2]

‚ÄúS√≠‚Äù

‚Äù).

‚ÄúS√≠‚Äù
¬†y contiene t√©rminos como ‚Äú
significant
 
impact
‚Äù, ‚Äú

‚Äù, ‚Äú

 decline‚Äù, etc., env√≠a una alerta v√≠a

¬†o

- El t√≠tulo del art√≠culo 
- Enlace

¬†T√©cnico, acad√©mico y objetivo.

class 
PDFReport
(FPDF):
    def header(self):
        
self.set_font
('Arial', 'B', 15)
        
self.cell
(0, 10, 'Reporte de Literatura Cient√≠fica', 0, 1, 'C')
        
self.ln
(10)
    
    def 
chapter_title
(self, title):
        
self.set_font
('Arial', 'B', 12)
        
self.cell
(0, 10, title, 0, 1, 'L')
        
self.ln
(4)
    
    def 
chapter_body
(self, body):
        
self.set_font
('Arial', '', 10)
        
self.multi_cell
(0, 8, body)
        
self.ln
()
# 
Cliente
 
Supabase
@st.cache_resource
def 
init_supabase
():
    return 
create_client
(
        
st.secrets
["SUPABASE_URL"],
        
st.secrets
["SUPABASE_KEY"]
    )
# 
Funciones
 
principales
def trigger_n8n_workflow(topic, 
start_date
, 
end_date
):
    
"""Dispara el 
workflow
 de n8n con los par√°metros del usuario"""
    
    
n8n_webhook_url = 
st.secrets
["N8N_WEBHOOK_URL"]
    
    payload = {
        "topic": topic,
        "
start_date
": 
start_date.isoformat
(),
        "
end_date
": 
end_date.isoformat
(),
        "
execution_id
": 
f"streamlit
_{int(
time.time
())}"
    }
    
    try:
        response = 
requests.post
(n8n_webhook_url, 
json
=payload, timeout=30)
        if 
response.status_code
 == 200:
            return True, "Workflow 
iniciado
 
correctamente
"
        else:
            return False, 
f"Error
 
en
 n8n: {
response.status_code
}"
    except Exception as e:
        
return
 False, 
f"Error
 conectando con n8n: {
str
(e)}"
def 
fetch_papers_from_supabase
(
topic_filter
=None, 
date_range
=None):
    
"""Obtiene 
papers
 de 
Supabase
 con filtros"""
    
supabase
 = 
init_supabase
()
    
    query = 
supabase.table
('papers').select('*').order('
created_at
', desc=True)
    
    if 
topic_filter
:
        query = 
query.ilike
('title', f'%{
topic_filter
}%')
    
    if 
date_range
:
        
start_date
, 
end_date
 = 
date_range
        query = 
query.gte
('
created_at
', 
start_date.isoformat
()).
lte
('
created_at
', 
end_date.isoformat
())
    
    response = 
query.execute
()
    return 
pd.DataFrame
(
response.data
) if 
response.data
 else 
pd.DataFrame
()
def 
generate_descriptive_stats
(
df
):
    
"""Genera 
estad√≠sticas
 
descriptivas
"""
    if 
df.empty
:
        
return {}
    
    stats = {
        '
total_papers
': 
len
(
df
),
        '
relevant_papers
': 
len
(
df
[
df
['relevant'] == '
S√≠
']),
        '

': (
len
(
df
[
df
['relevant'] == '
S√≠
']) / 
len
(
df
)) * 100 if 
len
(
df
) &gt; 0 else 0,
        '

': 
df
['
publication_year
'].
value_counts
().

(),
        '
recent_papers
': 
len
(
df
[
df
['
created_at
'] &gt;= (
datetime.now
() - 
timedelta
(days=7)).
isoformat
()])
    }
    return stats
def

(

, stats):
    
"""

    if

# Gr√°fico de relevancia

)

    #

    if

        fig2 =

    else:

    # Gr√°fico de evoluci√≥n temporal de procesamiento

    fig3 =

    return fig1, fig2, fig3
def

(

, stats, topic,

):
    
"""Genera reporte PDF completo"""

(
)

    # Informaci√≥n del an√°lisis

('Arial', 'B', 10)

f"T√≠tulo

('title', 'N/A')}", 0, 1)

            authors =

            else:

f"Hallazgos

    #

    if

-- 
Tabla
 principal de papers
CREATE TABLE papers (
    
id UUID DEFAULT 
gen_random_
uuid
(
) PRIMARY KEY,
    title TEXT NOT NULL,
    authors JSONB,
    
publication_year
 INTEGER,
    
doi
 TEXT,
    
url
 TEXT,
    abstract TEXT,
    venue TEXT,
    
citation_count
 INTEGER,
    relevant TEXT CHECK (relevant IN ('
S√≠
', 'No')),
    summary TEXT,
    
key_findings
 TEXT,
    
execution_id
 TEXT,
    
search_topic
 TEXT,
    
processed_at
 TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    
created_at
 TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT 
NOW(
)
);
-- 
√çndices
 para 
optimizaci√≥n
CREATE INDEX 
idx_papers_relevant
 ON papers(relevant);
CREATE INDEX 
idx_papers_topic
 ON papers(
search_topic
);
CREATE INDEX 
idx_papers_year
 ON papers(
publication_year
);
CREATE INDEX 
idx_papers_created_at
 ON papers(
created_at
);
CREATE INDEX 
idx_papers_execution
 ON papers(
execution_id
);
-- Vista para 
estad√≠sticas
CREATE VIEW 
paper_stats
 AS
SELECT 
    
search_topic
,
    COUNT(*) as 
total_papers
,
    COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE relevant = '
S√≠
') as 
relevant_papers
,
    ROUND((
COUNT(
*) FILTER (WHERE relevant = '
S√≠
') * 100.0 / COUNT(*)), 2) as 
relevance_rate
,
    
AVG(
publication_year
) as 
avg_publication_year
,
    
MAX(
processed_at
) as 
last_processed
FROM papers
GROUP BY 
search_topic
;

sql
-- Tabla principal de 
papers
CREATE TABLE papers (
    
id UUID DEFAULT 
gen_random_
uuid
(
) PRIMARY KEY,
    title TEXT NOT NULL,
    authors JSONB,
    
publication_year
 INTEGER,
    
doi
 TEXT,
    
url
 TEXT,
    abstract TEXT,
    venue TEXT,
    
citation_count
 INTEGER,
    relevant TEXT CHECK (relevant IN ('
S√≠
', 'No')),
    summary TEXT,
    
key_findings
 TEXT,
    
execution_id
 TEXT,
    
search_topic
 TEXT,
    
search_date_range
 TEXT,
    
processed_at
 TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT 
NOW(
),
    
created_at
 TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT 
NOW(
)
);
-- 
√çndices
 para 
optimizaci√≥n
CREATE INDEX 
idx_papers_relevant
 ON papers(relevant);
CREATE INDEX 
idx_papers_topic
 ON papers(
search_topic
);
CREATE INDEX 
idx_papers_year
 ON papers(
publication_year
);
CREATE INDEX 
idx_papers_created_at
 ON papers(
created_at
);
CREATE INDEX 
idx_papers_execution
 ON papers(
execution_id
);
-- Vista para 
estad√≠sticas
CREATE VIEW 
paper_stats
 AS
SELECT 
    
search_topic
,
    COUNT(*) as 
total_papers
,
    COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE relevant = '
S√≠
') as 
relevant_papers
,
    ROUND((
COUNT(
*) FILTER (WHERE relevant = '
S√≠
') * 100.0 / COUNT(*)), 2) as 
relevance_rate
,
    
AVG(
publication_year
) as 
avg_publication_year
,
    
MAX(
processed_at
) as 
last_processed
FROM papers
GROUP BY 
search_topic
;
